<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Music in the Cue</h2><a id="user-content-music-in-the-cue" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Music in the Cue" href="#music-in-the-cue"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Using music in the cue it's one way to enhance the performance that you record</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128659087-68664d28-833c-467e-9c87-fcebdb541485.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128659087-68664d28-833c-467e-9c87-fcebdb541485.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-08 at 23 00 42" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">FX in the Cue</h2><a id="user-content-fx-in-the-cue" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: FX in the Cue" href="#fx-in-the-cue"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If a Bus is Post-Fader (Default) then if you lower the volume of the origin is not going to send much audio to the aux track</p>
<p dir="auto">Selecting the PRE button will make the bus to be Pre-Fader</p>
<p dir="auto">Using Pre-Fader bus you can lower the volume of the original voice and just hear the processed output</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128659579-4a5e4031-333a-46d3-baa9-3ffd1a63a457.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128659579-4a5e4031-333a-46d3-baa9-3ffd1a63a457.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-08 at 23 08 57" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Breathless</h2><a id="user-content-breathless" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Breathless" href="#breathless"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can cut and remove the duplicates in Shuffle Mode to make a dialog that looks like there were no pauses to take a breath</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128660670-44717af6-db0b-4e97-b70c-33f2761d1885.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128660670-44717af6-db0b-4e97-b70c-33f2761d1885.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-08 at 23 32 54" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">The TCE Trimmer</h2><a id="user-content-the-tce-trimmer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: The TCE Trimmer" href="#the-tce-trimmer"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">TCE Trimmer = Time Expansion and Compression Trimmer</p>
<p dir="auto">Right Click the Trimer Icon and you'll see this options</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128660972-b116281c-6417-421b-a943-11e9c613c9ef.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128660972-b116281c-6417-421b-a943-11e9c613c9ef.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-08 at 23 39 05" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">If you use this trimmer it will make the audio go faster or slower</p>
<p dir="auto">In the Clip Bin you'll see the original and the Timeshifted version</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128661193-bfc16b5b-237d-4884-8c92-b235bc5a3486.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128661193-bfc16b5b-237d-4884-8c92-b235bc5a3486.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-08 at 23 43 13" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Editing Music Tracks</h1><a id="user-content-editing-music-tracks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Editing Music Tracks" href="#editing-music-tracks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Editing Library Music</h2><a id="user-content-editing-library-music" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Editing Library Music" href="#editing-library-music"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Remember that you can you <code>Option + Click</code> to disable timeline info that's not useful</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662141-81fc7e37-d10f-483f-a2e6-9d3e1ea79ac6.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662141-81fc7e37-d10f-483f-a2e6-9d3e1ea79ac6.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 03 34" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>How to measure Tempo</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Option 1 - Tap Tempo</p>
<p dir="auto">If keyboard focus is off</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662562-5d90ceb4-d0c2-4507-ba62-9bfe3b1722c4.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662562-5d90ceb4-d0c2-4507-ba62-9bfe3b1722c4.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 08 34" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">And the conductor is inactive (Transport Window)</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662606-b6885390-9158-41cf-a45a-4ad0699705a7.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662606-b6885390-9158-41cf-a45a-4ad0699705a7.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 09 39" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can actually control the tempo</p>
<p dir="auto">Setup &gt; Preferences &gt; MIDI &gt; Use MIDI to Tap Tempo</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662815-221e4bdc-acbe-4f15-82f1-d4b9c3d7e85a.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662815-221e4bdc-acbe-4f15-82f1-d4b9c3d7e85a.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 13 44" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can use letter T while the tempo is highlighted</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662830-941e5a08-7431-407d-b737-7f09a8203b8b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128662830-941e5a08-7431-407d-b737-7f09a8203b8b.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 14 08" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Using Identify Beat</h2><a id="user-content-using-identify-beat" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Using Identify Beat" href="#using-identify-beat"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Option 2 - Identify Beat</p>
<p dir="auto">Enable Conductor</p>
<p dir="auto">Select where the 2nd bar should be and use <code>Command + I</code></p>
<p dir="auto">And set the value to 2|1|000</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128663424-c780f338-0758-452e-8171-6e5987f488d7.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128663424-c780f338-0758-452e-8171-6e5987f488d7.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 24 39" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select where the 3th bar should be and use <code>Command + I</code></p>
<p dir="auto">And set the value to 3|1|000</p>
<p dir="auto">Select where the 4th bar should be and use <code>Command + I</code></p>
<p dir="auto">And set the value to 4|1|000</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Slicing Music using the Grid</h2><a id="user-content-slicing-music-using-the-grid" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Slicing Music using the Grid" href="#slicing-music-using-the-grid"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Option 3 -</p>
<p dir="auto">Enable Grid Mode</p>
<p dir="auto">Select 1/8 in the Grid Value</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664058-603c3be3-6900-45c9-a2d9-382944480557.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664058-603c3be3-6900-45c9-a2d9-382944480557.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 37 08" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Highlight the Tempo and scroll until you see it's aligned</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664164-0d2a322a-2d4c-4113-b309-4c6a76fc4a22.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664164-0d2a322a-2d4c-4113-b309-4c6a76fc4a22.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 38 45" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Use Grid Mode to Select, <code>Command + D</code> to duplicate your selection</p>
<p dir="auto">Select the duplicates using Grid Mode, move to Shuffle Mode and move them at the beginning</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664585-b30341cc-4232-4cb4-8fca-371b71e8268b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664585-b30341cc-4232-4cb4-8fca-371b71e8268b.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 47 29" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Put Grid 1/4 Notes</p>
<p dir="auto">Select All</p>
<p dir="auto">Edit &gt; Separate Clip &gt; On Grid</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664883-59ae40da-6898-4aec-8bdc-94d60bcf5ef1.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/128664883-59ae40da-6898-4aec-8bdc-94d60bcf5ef1.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-09 at 0 52 30" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Splices and Crossfades</h2><a id="user-content-splices-and-crossfades" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Splices and Crossfades" href="#splices-and-crossfades"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Import audio files and put 123 as tempo</p>
<p dir="auto">Go to Bar 9, and select it in Grid Mode, Command + E to cut it, and rename it as "Intro"</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131239686-434c9bac-d6f3-4dcd-a667-2ef3ca9d2cce.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131239686-434c9bac-d6f3-4dcd-a667-2ef3ca9d2cce.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 29 18" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Move to Shuffle Mode, and drag it to the beginning, Command + D to add 3 more of those</p>
<p dir="auto">Add crossfades between the repeated intros we added</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131239924-b6aac66a-4099-44eb-b39c-bd05e45ce5dd.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131239924-b6aac66a-4099-44eb-b39c-bd05e45ce5dd.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 40 41" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can also Fade Down after the intros:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240030-0fa7b2f8-bd34-4c7e-b346-ece7098ffa25.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240030-0fa7b2f8-bd34-4c7e-b346-ece7098ffa25.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 44 14" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Switch to Grid Mode</p>
<p dir="auto">Move the first audio track to Bar 5:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240094-ee33459d-44ce-46aa-9411-2ee21b31b508.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240094-ee33459d-44ce-46aa-9411-2ee21b31b508.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 46 36" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Now mute the clip with Command + M:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240132-0ac9af6a-5562-42ae-a5fd-0fe968edd5c6.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240132-0ac9af6a-5562-42ae-a5fd-0fe968edd5c6.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 48 17" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select the Upper Track, change Tempo to 96</p>
<p dir="auto">You can select Bar 5 and Option + Drag will duplicate the Bar</p>
<p dir="auto">Fade In the Upper Track, Full One Bar Fade In</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240256-b7f422f5-4dec-4fdf-81be-e4840869453e.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240256-b7f422f5-4dec-4fdf-81be-e4840869453e.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 53 36" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">And Full Bar Fade Out in the Lower Track</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240322-490a80d0-3012-4ab5-b04b-f9a78760197f.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240322-490a80d0-3012-4ab5-b04b-f9a78760197f.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 57 15" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240355-164dd920-6993-4f46-b575-3bbf8116eb65.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240355-164dd920-6993-4f46-b575-3bbf8116eb65.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 0 58 51" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Consolidate VS Bounce</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Consolidate will give us each track independently</li>
<li>Bounce will give us the combination of the tracks</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Select from End to Beginning what you want to bounce</p>
<p dir="auto">File &gt; Bounce &gt; To Disk</p>
<p dir="auto">Format: Interleaved
Check Offline</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Fade and Crossfade Options</h2><a id="user-content-fade-and-crossfade-options" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Fade and Crossfade Options" href="#fade-and-crossfade-options"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Setup &gt; Preferences &gt; Editing &gt; Fades</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240866-be860e01-5a53-43e7-9631-efabe3067dd0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240866-be860e01-5a53-43e7-9631-efabe3067dd0.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 25 45" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can change the curve of the Fade-Out, Fade-In or CrossFades:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240965-22c81943-894e-4790-bfed-f3f9835162bb.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240965-22c81943-894e-4790-bfed-f3f9835162bb.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 30 06" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240986-6f62d540-6049-4bdf-9725-2f3e39b6c0b5.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131240986-6f62d540-6049-4bdf-9725-2f3e39b6c0b5.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 31 07" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Edit &gt; Fades &gt; Create</p>
<p dir="auto">Even in a selection at the end, click Command + F to add a Fade Out</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241061-d8443334-9d2d-442c-976c-8c088edce604.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241061-d8443334-9d2d-442c-976c-8c088edce604.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 33 56" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241091-d1107d38-b037-4599-b235-d515a128633e.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241091-d1107d38-b037-4599-b235-d515a128633e.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 34 55" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Put the selector in the middle of a Clip</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241134-33feaae0-c143-40df-9505-465b2d2a2197.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241134-33feaae0-c143-40df-9505-465b2d2a2197.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 36 44" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Edit &gt; Fades &gt; Fade to Start</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241157-3d30d9b7-95e5-48e7-a9e9-b59ccd20a8c0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241157-3d30d9b7-95e5-48e7-a9e9-b59ccd20a8c0.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 37 44" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select other part</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241177-cccc3b69-b8e8-4937-af61-44cdcc4b7595.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131241177-cccc3b69-b8e8-4937-af61-44cdcc4b7595.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 1 38 31" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Changing Tempo of Library Music Tracks</h2><a id="user-content-changing-tempo-of-library-music-tracks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Changing Tempo of Library Music Tracks" href="#changing-tempo-of-library-music-tracks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Let's move our 123 Tempo track to 100</p>
<p dir="auto">Select the Track, put the Tempo to 100</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131242861-19e6b5a8-66b9-4be3-aa24-a28324d60b4a.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131242861-19e6b5a8-66b9-4be3-aa24-a28324d60b4a.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 2 47 06" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Change to Time Compressor</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131242623-f17bb200-2890-40cb-a3e2-42e8390098ef.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131242623-f17bb200-2890-40cb-a3e2-42e8390098ef.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 2 39 01" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131242881-f9de7d21-0d60-4107-826a-e9fe54c2a0e7.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131242881-f9de7d21-0d60-4107-826a-e9fe54c2a0e7.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 2 47 54" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Setting Triggers in Beat Detective</h2><a id="user-content-setting-triggers-in-beat-detective" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Setting Triggers in Beat Detective" href="#setting-triggers-in-beat-detective"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Event &gt; Tempo Operations &gt; Tempo Operations Window</p>
<p dir="auto">Select a Drum or Ritmic Track</p>
<p dir="auto">Event &gt; Beat Detective &gt; Analyze</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243289-e45de01c-e303-4296-8922-a67f3b35e0bc.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243289-e45de01c-e303-4296-8922-a67f3b35e0bc.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 03 18" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Adjust the Sensitivity to get the correct amount of bars</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243465-06bd66cc-2b77-4344-bdcf-3dbdf11002af.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243465-06bd66cc-2b77-4344-bdcf-3dbdf11002af.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 10 40" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can manually adjust the bars in case of misdetection</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243602-0f76dc1d-905f-4f43-8ed9-246b0a112272.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243602-0f76dc1d-905f-4f43-8ed9-246b0a112272.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 16 22" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Conforming Trigger in Beat Detective</h2><a id="user-content-conforming-trigger-in-beat-detective" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conforming Trigger in Beat Detective" href="#conforming-trigger-in-beat-detective"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">After detecting the Beats correctly</p>
<p dir="auto">Select "Clip Separation" &gt; Separate</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243656-4511f15f-152a-4cd0-9795-0e6f915f9d42.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243656-4511f15f-152a-4cd0-9795-0e6f915f9d42.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 18 11" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Event &gt; Tempo Operations &gt; Tempo Operations Window</p>
<p dir="auto">Change from 100 to 105 Tempo</p>
<p dir="auto">Select "Clip Conform" &gt; Conform</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243870-e3e80d01-d45e-4f4b-8ddd-d18c8f6b58ae.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243870-e3e80d01-d45e-4f4b-8ddd-d18c8f6b58ae.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 25 45" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You could also try to change it to 95 Tempo</p>
<p dir="auto">Event &gt; Tempo Operations &gt; Tempo Operations Window</p>
<p dir="auto">Change from 100 to 95 Tempo</p>
<p dir="auto">Select "Clip Conform" &gt; Conform</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243985-7787ecf8-f5b5-4857-a37d-18d4ac3735ec.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131243985-7787ecf8-f5b5-4857-a37d-18d4ac3735ec.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 30 13" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">But we have some gaps between the clips</p>
<p dir="auto">Select "Edit Smoothing" &gt; Smooth</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131244115-701248bb-4baf-4f88-b8df-ccb98d93df4f.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131244115-701248bb-4baf-4f88-b8df-ccb98d93df4f.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 32 29" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Let's try "Fill and Crossfade"</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131244206-5870c04e-1002-4ed6-9ee1-eb7f8bee62ec.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131244206-5870c04e-1002-4ed6-9ee1-eb7f8bee62ec.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 3 35 22" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Elastic Audio</h1><a id="user-content-elastic-audio" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Elastic Audio" href="#elastic-audio"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Elastic Audio for a Voice Track</h2><a id="user-content-elastic-audio-for-a-voice-track" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Elastic Audio for a Voice Track" href="#elastic-audio-for-a-voice-track"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are the algorithms available for elastic audio
These 3 doesn't affect the pitch:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Polyphonic - when you have more than one tone at the same time (chords)</li>
<li>Rhythmic - when you don't have any pitches</li>
<li>Monophonic - just one voice
These one will not only change the timing but also the speed</li>
<li>Varispeed</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131259644-fc3aa7d6-a995-46d1-9a09-76caea3c501f.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131259644-fc3aa7d6-a995-46d1-9a09-76caea3c501f.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 29 22" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">If you select Monophonic and change from Waveform to Analysis, you should see something like this:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131259841-f322535d-48c2-41e1-91ed-e8e8eaa23a50.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131259841-f322535d-48c2-41e1-91ed-e8e8eaa23a50.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 34 40" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">There are more markers than we want, so we can adjust markers and Option + Click to remove a marker</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131259993-0ea3ec54-c0b5-460b-b21d-c42cc7985163.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131259993-0ea3ec54-c0b5-460b-b21d-c42cc7985163.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 39 11" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">That's the Analysis, now we can move to Warp</p>
<p dir="auto">Double-Click to add an Anchor Point</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260057-4d96d036-9007-43fe-9818-c9a0b557d026.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260057-4d96d036-9007-43fe-9818-c9a0b557d026.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 41 28" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">And now you can stretch:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260079-5cddaa9c-2331-4746-8a42-494f169174b3.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260079-5cddaa9c-2331-4746-8a42-494f169174b3.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 42 09" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We notice the Monophonic sounds robotic, so we can to Polyphonic and it sounds better</p>
<p dir="auto">You'll know if Elastic Audio was applied to a Clip because of that icon:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260223-0a0a8834-41fd-4e2f-8d32-4ec88eea2801.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260223-0a0a8834-41fd-4e2f-8d32-4ec88eea2801.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 45 57" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260254-24870d3e-4bca-4d4c-a487-4176ac27d378.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260254-24870d3e-4bca-4d4c-a487-4176ac27d378.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 47 14" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Elastic Audio for Music</h2><a id="user-content-elastic-audio-for-music" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Elastic Audio for Music" href="#elastic-audio-for-music"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We want to keep the Kick Parts and move the Snare Parts</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260381-fc942c9b-1beb-4609-9945-c794cc85216d.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260381-fc942c9b-1beb-4609-9945-c794cc85216d.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 52 00" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">In this case we will use Rhythmic algorithm</p>
<p dir="auto">Track &gt; Create Click Track</p>
<p dir="auto">You can Enable/Disable the Click with that icon in Transport Window</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260450-9910f287-8e32-4e37-9fad-4333983b35dc.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260450-9910f287-8e32-4e37-9fad-4333983b35dc.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 54 26" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Now we switch to Analysis</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260504-272aeb1d-d991-426b-afe4-c71001cf8a90.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260504-272aeb1d-d991-426b-afe4-c71001cf8a90.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 56 06" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We move to Warp and start Anchoring the good parts</p>
<p dir="auto">It's easier if we move to Grid Mode and we are sure that the grid is a 1/4 note</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260615-070d9b6d-2421-48b6-aacc-b6e5ffceb425.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260615-070d9b6d-2421-48b6-aacc-b6e5ffceb425.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 12 59 41" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260661-797d3d53-5a24-4827-99da-6430ee6c12f7.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260661-797d3d53-5a24-4827-99da-6430ee6c12f7.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 00 47" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Pitch Adjustments using Elastic Audio</h2><a id="user-content-pitch-adjustments-using-elastic-audio" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Pitch Adjustments using Elastic Audio" href="#pitch-adjustments-using-elastic-audio"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Clip &gt; Elastic Properties</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260798-20459be8-3477-41ae-9d88-44274da5c443.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260798-20459be8-3477-41ae-9d88-44274da5c443.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 05 52" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select the Clip using Polyphonic and you would be able to change Pitch Shift Positive/Negative</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260884-c8adb48d-ef20-4268-9fb5-4e81f0043ad5.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131260884-c8adb48d-ef20-4268-9fb5-4e81f0043ad5.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 08 06" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adding Rhythm Guitar</h2><a id="user-content-adding-rhythm-guitar" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Adding Rhythm Guitar" href="#adding-rhythm-guitar"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a Project from "Songwriter - Guitarist" Template</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261592-6e984870-8500-42f4-b60a-89d1fa32aac7.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261592-6e984870-8500-42f4-b60a-89d1fa32aac7.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 36 25" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Open Mix Window, select first Track</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261637-c928c896-d34d-4f28-97fb-f48eee97a00d.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261637-c928c896-d34d-4f28-97fb-f48eee97a00d.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 37 48" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Then press Shift and select last Track; that will select all the tracks</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261661-f1bc7a8d-1bc2-4f1f-9c62-4da4eb75f099.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261661-f1bc7a8d-1bc2-4f1f-9c62-4da4eb75f099.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 38 50" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Command and click headphone to deselect it</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261713-3d2a3353-8c8b-449c-a8d5-bd7e7e57c745.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261713-3d2a3353-8c8b-449c-a8d5-bd7e7e57c745.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 40 20" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Press Shift + Control + Option</p>
<p dir="auto">Select an output and that will apply it to all the Tracks</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261790-332fb362-5899-4175-a7fe-f7d49a016e1e.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261790-332fb362-5899-4175-a7fe-f7d49a016e1e.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 42 58" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Now let's record a guitar:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261966-1cd988e4-1aeb-4e54-8178-232536f3b214.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131261966-1cd988e4-1aeb-4e54-8178-232536f3b214.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 47 48" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Arranging using the Timeline</h2><a id="user-content-arranging-using-the-timeline" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Arranging using the Timeline" href="#arranging-using-the-timeline"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Let's say we want an intro, so let's move the drums and guitar to Bar 5:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262016-857da265-3da6-4d7c-b98f-004c3e8e8146.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262016-857da265-3da6-4d7c-b98f-004c3e8e8146.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 49 54" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Use the Loop Trimmer, that shows automatically if you have a loop in the timeline</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262089-5f72e228-6a07-49e2-8540-13e9c2872455.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262089-5f72e228-6a07-49e2-8540-13e9c2872455.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 52 24" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can open by Double-Clicking the Drum Clip, select the notes you want to Mute and press Command + M</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262105-2d0f3f71-8a77-43f6-a2f8-d246b7ac2ce6.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262105-2d0f3f71-8a77-43f6-a2f8-d246b7ac2ce6.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 53 02" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Count Off gives you two Bars before recording so you can prepare:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262162-6918ecb9-cfd4-4bc9-8b0d-b869fd6e1c22.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262162-6918ecb9-cfd4-4bc9-8b0d-b869fd6e1c22.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 55 10" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can change that in Setup &gt; Click/Countoff</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262227-b0cb8c63-d0bb-484f-9a30-383ce1edc399.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262227-b0cb8c63-d0bb-484f-9a30-383ce1edc399.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 57 47" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Now let's record the intro for the Guitar:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262292-bd02b7db-76e2-4a71-89a8-f20257725628.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262292-bd02b7db-76e2-4a71-89a8-f20257725628.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 13 59 09" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">And add a crossfade if necessary</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Guitar Amp Simulators</h2><a id="user-content-guitar-amp-simulators" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Guitar Amp Simulators" href="#guitar-amp-simulators"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Go to Mix Windows and to the Guitar Effects</p>
<p dir="auto">Eleven Lite:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262356-c0d11766-228d-4db3-b160-e7365c0e0860.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262356-c0d11766-228d-4db3-b160-e7365c0e0860.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 03 13" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">PSA-1:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262413-0ee1e4e6-d9e5-4ca9-aedc-f00438ea2f9e.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262413-0ee1e4e6-d9e5-4ca9-aedc-f00438ea2f9e.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 06 15" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Loop Record and Playlists</h2><a id="user-content-loop-record-and-playlists" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Loop Record and Playlists" href="#loop-record-and-playlists"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Select 4 Bars that you want to record:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262635-bf7763fd-6bfd-4c3a-9df8-3948022f9bf6.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262635-bf7763fd-6bfd-4c3a-9df8-3948022f9bf6.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 13 09" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Options &gt; Loop Record</p>
<p dir="auto">You'll see that now Playback and Record have the Loop icon:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262666-0700e445-6aee-44d8-8cd2-63cd8cd7821c.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262666-0700e445-6aee-44d8-8cd2-63cd8cd7821c.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 14 49" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Click in the inverted triangle and you'll see all the recordings:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262747-3014c594-56b8-49c8-8f57-8292d5c5473a.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262747-3014c594-56b8-49c8-8f57-8292d5c5473a.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 17 31" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Comping a Playlist</h2><a id="user-content-comping-a-playlist" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Comping a Playlist" href="#comping-a-playlist"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can also see the waveform of all the recordings in the Playlist:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262799-c6f18051-3362-482d-8beb-d8e8e9c91881.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262799-c6f18051-3362-482d-8beb-d8e8e9c91881.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 19 27" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262820-be3e132a-fbcd-4f24-851b-0046e61f1873.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262820-be3e132a-fbcd-4f24-851b-0046e61f1873.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 20 27" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select Grid Mode and 1/4 notes</p>
<p dir="auto">You can select a part and elevate it:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262847-11d9e674-df07-479e-be32-23f58482379d.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131262847-11d9e674-df07-479e-be32-23f58482379d.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 21 43" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Punch</h2><a id="user-content-quick-punch" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Punch" href="#quick-punch"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Check these options:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263006-12be5af9-ff47-42b7-b9ec-8a0b3c5b0622.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263006-12be5af9-ff47-42b7-b9ec-8a0b3c5b0622.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 28 22" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Disable Loop Recording</p>
<p dir="auto">You can set an Start and End points for recording:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263038-fbd5486c-7012-49cc-939f-6c21537dc45b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263038-fbd5486c-7012-49cc-939f-6c21537dc45b.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 29 24" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263065-6126e80c-b115-4526-bc99-4b8381604228.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263065-6126e80c-b115-4526-bc99-4b8381604228.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 30 20" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Options &gt; Quick Punch</p>
<p dir="auto">Now you can use F12 to stop recording</p>
<p dir="auto">This will for example give a new bar 9 but keep original bar 10</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263082-009ab6f1-a9c9-4d8a-93db-dc41f5d6327f.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263082-009ab6f1-a9c9-4d8a-93db-dc41f5d6327f.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 31 25" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Or record some part, keep the original part and recording a new part after</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263126-d90aff9e-8b1c-44cc-be30-aa8b1ce9e2b5.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263126-d90aff9e-8b1c-44cc-be30-aa8b1ce9e2b5.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 33 29" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dynamic Transport</h2><a id="user-content-dynamic-transport" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dynamic Transport" href="#dynamic-transport"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Options &gt; Dynamic Transport</p>
<p dir="auto">You can set Bar 6 as reference and jump to Bar 10 to Record:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263609-d8882e9f-1677-4980-9378-992f29224a63.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131263609-d8882e9f-1677-4980-9378-992f29224a63.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 14 53 02" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">And you can combine it with Quick Punch</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Half Speed Recording</h2><a id="user-content-half-speed-recording" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Half Speed Recording" href="#half-speed-recording"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Shift + Command + Space = Half Speed Recording</p>
<p dir="auto">You'll have a record with the speed doubled and a higher pitch</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">The Philosophy of Mixing</h2><a id="user-content-the-philosophy-of-mixing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: The Philosophy of Mixing" href="#the-philosophy-of-mixing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create a Session with "24+EQ+Dyn+FX Returns" Template (Record+Mix Category)</p>
<p dir="auto">The beauty of mix is in how the sounds blend and compliment one another and not how a single instrument sound by itself</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">EQ and Volume</h2><a id="user-content-eq-and-volume" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: EQ and Volume" href="#eq-and-volume"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Volume - OPTION 1</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Anytime you have more than 1 Track happenning at the same time you want a Master Fader</p>
<p dir="auto">The idea is to move individual faders so that you can leave the Master Fader at 0, and have the peak from -3 to 0.3</p>
<p dir="auto">RECOMMENDATION: Line the tracks up in their orden of importance</p>
<p dir="auto">If your tracks were recorded right your faders are going to be loud, a little softer, a little softer ...</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>EQ - OPTION 2</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Another option is to carve out a space in the frequency spectrum that lets that part stand out</p>
<p dir="auto">Let's say you want the guitar to have more presence in the middle frequencies; rather than boost the middle frequencies of the guitar try reducing those same frequencies in the bass</p>
<p dir="auto">If two sounds are fighting one another, try EQ</p>
<p dir="auto">You can boost the good stuff or cut the bad stuff</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131269875-bfc7ae6a-8b93-4e87-90b7-4e47ddcf403b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131269875-bfc7ae6a-8b93-4e87-90b7-4e47ddcf403b.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 19 07 10" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Thinking about the texture of each element:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Does it need Reverb?</li>
<li>Does it need Delay?</li>
<li>Does it need Compression?</li>
<li>Is the Volume perfect from End to End?</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Busses, Sends, Auxes and Inserts</h2><a id="user-content-busses-sends-auxes-and-inserts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Busses, Sends, Auxes and Inserts" href="#busses-sends-auxes-and-inserts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">These are some effects that are common for a Pop Song:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270044-d670e8e8-b485-4e51-9679-390f03c06667.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270044-d670e8e8-b485-4e51-9679-390f03c06667.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 19 12 34" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Verb - AIR Reverb</li>
<li>Slap - ModDelay 3, Lo-Fi (Harmonic Section), EQ3 1-Band</li>
<li>StereoDel1</li>
<li>ChurchVerb</li>
<li>Master 1</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto">ModDelay 3</p>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270395-ce316632-afdc-41a0-90db-a65353cb6c1b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270395-ce316632-afdc-41a0-90db-a65353cb6c1b.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 19 23 38" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<p dir="auto">If the tile is blue it means is bypassed</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270432-4961944e-0851-46d1-8a3e-0e4b2d22ade2.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270432-4961944e-0851-46d1-8a3e-0e4b2d22ade2.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 19 24 40" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">If it's red it means the Send Level has been exceeded , there's been digital clipping</p>
<p dir="auto">Transport Windows &gt; Fade-in (it saves you from having an instant full volume when you hit play)</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Panning, Marker Locations and the Universe</h2><a id="user-content-panning-marker-locations-and-the-universe" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Panning, Marker Locations and the Universe" href="#panning-marker-locations-and-the-universe"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Panning</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">It's important to equilibrate the panning and not just have it at 100 left and right in Stereo, and at the center if it's Mono</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270609-fa800e86-2239-49b2-b098-d658f8c68715.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/131270609-fa800e86-2239-49b2-b098-d658f8c68715.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-08-29 at 19 29 28" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
