<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Automating Volume, Pan and Send Levels</h2><a id="user-content-automating-volume-pan-and-send-levels" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Automating Volume, Pan and Send Levels" href="#automating-volume-pan-and-send-levels"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">VOLUME Automation</h3><a id="user-content-volume-automation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: VOLUME Automation" href="#volume-automation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Auto Write</h4><a id="user-content-auto-write" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Auto Write" href="#auto-write"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">1.- Go from "auto read" to "auto write"</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134793934-1c2dcc4a-c2a1-4099-8bc6-46fe76f1e923.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134793934-1c2dcc4a-c2a1-4099-8bc6-46fe76f1e923.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-25 at 23 40 32" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">2.- Hit space bar to start playing</p>
<p dir="auto">3.- Make a volume move</p>
<p dir="auto">4.- The button changes to "auto latch"</p>
<p dir="auto">(if it's not switching to latch):
Setup &gt; Preferences &gt; Mixing &gt; Automation &gt; After Write Pass, Switch To: Latch</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134793982-3505c838-666d-4952-8841-cafe1a50a29a.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134793982-3505c838-666d-4952-8841-cafe1a50a29a.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-25 at 23 44 11" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">latch - in case you want the fader where you left it</p>
<p dir="auto">touch - in case you want the fader where it was originally</p>
<p dir="auto">There's the volume move:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794269-6a9b257e-6225-43e3-9b4e-e4d60cbce08c.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794269-6a9b257e-6225-43e3-9b4e-e4d60cbce08c.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-25 at 23 57 32" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">PANNING Automation</h3><a id="user-content-panning-automation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: PANNING Automation" href="#panning-automation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Jump to Edit Window</p>
<p dir="auto">Go "auto read"</p>
<p dir="auto">Add another line with the panning</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794459-6aa3506a-c4a5-4f63-a952-b03a83e75b02.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794459-6aa3506a-c4a5-4f63-a952-b03a83e75b02.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 0 06 02" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>PENCIL Automation</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Use the Pencil Tool</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794479-2c79de59-c949-4f06-bcf1-04dfbce766ae.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794479-2c79de59-c949-4f06-bcf1-04dfbce766ae.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 0 06 58" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select Line</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794496-ca3dcb1c-4ea4-4609-9246-ef92c9cca608.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794496-ca3dcb1c-4ea4-4609-9246-ef92c9cca608.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 0 07 28" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Start writing some lines in the pannning</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794529-479704d3-bb6c-42ad-aa88-802a38dd350b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794529-479704d3-bb6c-42ad-aa88-802a38dd350b.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 0 08 38" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">You can reduce the points in the automations by:
Edit &gt; Thin Automation</p>
<p dir="auto">Select the Automation</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794567-f102d65a-254f-4649-aafd-e4521d27c6fc.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794567-f102d65a-254f-4649-aafd-e4521d27c6fc.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 0 10 37" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Edit &gt; Thin Automation</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>FADER Automation</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Change to "auto write"</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794629-0345affa-1ff5-488c-8fbe-134104453bad.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794629-0345affa-1ff5-488c-8fbe-134104453bad.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 0 14 02" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Play and start writing the panning</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794644-b334c08b-0eb7-4ed5-a243-2fc5645d7c00.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134794644-b334c08b-0eb7-4ed5-a243-2fc5645d7c00.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 0 14 33" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Automating the Panning will erase the automation of the Volume
So if you want to automate particular items we can enable and disable those</p>
<p dir="auto">Jump to the Mix Window</p>
<p dir="auto">If you want to record automation during the recording process:</p>
<p dir="auto">Setup &gt; Preferences &gt; Operation &gt; Record &gt; Enable Automation in Record</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797482-83c0c9b2-dbb8-4a9f-ab02-7e3af21191b2.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797482-83c0c9b2-dbb8-4a9f-ab02-7e3af21191b2.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 06 00" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Automating Plugin Parameters</h2><a id="user-content-automating-plugin-parameters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Automating Plugin Parameters" href="#automating-plugin-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Select "auto read"</p>
<p dir="auto">In the Mix Window add a "D-Verb" plugin:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797695-617478d8-3007-496e-816f-41716c5fe7a6.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797695-617478d8-3007-496e-816f-41716c5fe7a6.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 13 20" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797713-67deae1a-f563-4c19-91d1-ef492d682633.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797713-67deae1a-f563-4c19-91d1-ef492d682633.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 14 05" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Click in th auto icon:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797729-ea76f717-5b9c-43c0-89fd-0812b3a7ae75.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797729-ea76f717-5b9c-43c0-89fd-0812b3a7ae75.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 14 43" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">They are in the left:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797748-1aa18bdb-2088-41e2-8fb6-61f42cd66f2c.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797748-1aa18bdb-2088-41e2-8fb6-61f42cd66f2c.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 15 17" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Select the ones you want to automate, and move them to the right:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797783-4d073719-5107-4b97-ae7d-0c89b9cbc34d.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797783-4d073719-5107-4b97-ae7d-0c89b9cbc34d.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 16 02" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">After that they'll be colored green:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797798-cf34957d-7d70-4f5b-bd4a-3ef96ef7c1a3.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797798-cf34957d-7d70-4f5b-bd4a-3ef96ef7c1a3.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 16 35" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">If you change to "auto write", they'll be colored red:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797866-c65aecd0-9a42-4206-9a19-2afff8ea996e.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134797866-c65aecd0-9a42-4206-9a19-2afff8ea996e.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 18 36" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Be careful if you change the type of reverb in the middle of mix or even in tracking</p>
<p dir="auto">You'll likely hear a click as it changes the algorithm</p>
<p dir="auto">These are automatable, but you might want to just change it in a muted spot</p>
<p dir="auto">For example if you automate a change in the Decay of the Reverb</p>
<p dir="auto">You can see the automation in LongVerb &gt; Decay</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134798062-fecd999e-077a-420d-af92-070cf02fe4f5.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134798062-fecd999e-077a-420d-af92-070cf02fe4f5.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 2 25 40" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compression and Customing Templates</h2><a id="user-content-compression-and-customing-templates" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compression and Customing Templates" href="#compression-and-customing-templates"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Simple Limiter</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">20:1 is pretty agressive</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825839-dccf5bf8-e445-4c45-9126-78d7f18713db.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825839-dccf5bf8-e445-4c45-9126-78d7f18713db.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 17 09 09" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">**Gentle Limiting **</p>
<p dir="auto">100:1</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825869-15061ae0-1eb0-4fb2-abba-587cf124ac19.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825869-15061ae0-1eb0-4fb2-abba-587cf124ac19.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 17 11 04" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Hard Limiting</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">100:1</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825898-1fab43e2-1540-4031-b09a-bc3df35fb320.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825898-1fab43e2-1540-4031-b09a-bc3df35fb320.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 17 12 31" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Fatten</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">20:1</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825920-7d348d93-f7aa-4e75-b835-aa9429c696e0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825920-7d348d93-f7aa-4e75-b835-aa9429c696e0.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 17 13 13" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Pump</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">10:1</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825936-e26da6d5-acfa-4bb0-b5c9-32c9bd57ea97.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134825936-e26da6d5-acfa-4bb0-b5c9-32c9bd57ea97.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 17 13 57" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We've sort of flattened this whole thing out so that:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>the very soft stuff is now being amplified a lot</li>
<li>the very loud stuff isn't presumably loud at all</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">You have several settings for how aggresive you want to be with this:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134836908-bc1a04c5-97e1-4e4a-b764-9cdf4351ca2b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134836908-bc1a04c5-97e1-4e4a-b764-9cdf4351ca2b.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 21 28 01" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Control + Click: Mute Inserts</p>
<p dir="auto">The compression depends a lot on whether you plan to master or not</p>
<p dir="auto">If you're mixing and this is the final output then some compression is advisable</p>
<p dir="auto">If you're going to a Mastering Engineer and you use up all the headroom, you're locking your mastering engineers ability to do his job</p>
<p dir="auto">If your mastering leave about 6dB of headroom for your master, yoiu shouldn't compress a lot. Because the Mastering Compressor probably has a better multichannel commpressor than you do, probably has better monitors than you do. And if you compress a lot you're killing the dynamics and that's part of a mastering engineers job</p>
<p dir="auto">You can save a session as a Template:</p>
<p dir="auto">File &gt; Save As Template</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Printing Effects and Stems</h2><a id="user-content-printing-effects-and-stems" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Printing Effects and Stems" href="#printing-effects-and-stems"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Issue 1</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Let's say the master has a plugin which you don't have:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134838370-d9842221-3ab0-43e1-90e4-30c4fdbbe7d0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134838370-d9842221-3ab0-43e1-90e4-30c4fdbbe7d0.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 21 47 44" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We see this a lot; people use a plugin that they own and then they send the session to somebody who doesn't have that plugin</p>
<p dir="auto">And this is what happens, the plugin gets italicised</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Issue 2</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Sometimes you'll be tying up a lot of processing power of your computer by sending a bunch of tracks to a reverb or a delay or some other processing unit. and you'll be doing that every time you hit play</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Workaround</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The tip is to print the effects as an audio file</p>
<p dir="auto">In the old days we would solo the lead vocal, solo the effects and then bounce whatever was soloed and then import it</p>
<p dir="auto">That system works fine but as ProTools 11 we have the ability to route this bus to a track:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839047-89d360ab-ff1b-439e-8105-f4e6fe2d47ac.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839047-89d360ab-ff1b-439e-8105-f4e6fe2d47ac.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 21 56 27" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Or make a new track for it:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839082-3e6353a3-d2c7-45eb-9381-8e55fa21fd9c.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839082-3e6353a3-d2c7-45eb-9381-8e55fa21fd9c.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 21 57 02" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839179-c825f55c-979e-4a63-86c7-f6c3874b5298.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839179-c825f55c-979e-4a63-86c7-f6c3874b5298.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 21 58 12" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">The new track now is there, but we need to route it</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839282-d89921e8-ff6e-425b-b551-a86453ec65ca.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134839282-d89921e8-ff6e-425b-b551-a86453ec65ca.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 21 59 44" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We can use the same system when a client asks you for <strong>stems</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Stems are typically all the vocals from the front of the song to the back of the song, all the rhythm might be the drum part from the front of the song to the back of the song</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Archiving your Session</h2><a id="user-content-archiving-your-session" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Archiving your Session" href="#archiving-your-session"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Let's say that we perfected our mix, got the levels right, got the textures right. Everything sounds great. The client is happy and it's time to archive this session and move to the next project</p>
<p dir="auto">Go to Clips &gt; Select &gt; Unused</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840057-2b55bfbf-7782-4176-a25d-80962f5b222a.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840057-2b55bfbf-7782-4176-a25d-80962f5b222a.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 22 11 06" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">File &gt; Save Copy In ...</p>
<p dir="auto">Items to Copy &gt; Check "Audio Files" and "Root Plugin Settings Folder"</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840187-70b6b2af-dd70-4928-aea9-64a6fb46a31d.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840187-70b6b2af-dd70-4928-aea9-64a6fb46a31d.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 22 12 56" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Use the word "Archive" in the title somewhere so it's clear when you see it that was the final archive of this session</p>
<p dir="auto">Then go to Clips and clear the Unused Clips</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840411-4e341240-ea24-4eef-ab92-b622322adb5c.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840411-4e341240-ea24-4eef-ab92-b622322adb5c.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 22 15 50" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Remove - just remove the clips form the session, but keep the files in the hardrive
Delete - it's the efficient way to also remove the files from the hardrive</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840537-e961e878-047d-42c5-b960-8043ef2f95e0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/51218415/134840537-e961e878-047d-42c5-b960-8043ef2f95e0.png" alt="Screen Shot 2021-09-26 at 22 17 28" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Some Pages to find Plugins:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Avid - <a href="https://www.avid.com/avid-plugins-by-category" rel="nofollow">https://www.avid.com/avid-plugins-by-category</a></li>
